JavaScript/TypeScript code snippets from MDX documentation files.\n */\n\nimport fs from 'fs';\n\n/**\n * Represents a code snippet from documentation.\n */\nexport class CodeSnippet {\n    constructor(content, lineNumber, snippetId, language = 'javascript') {\n        this.content = content;\n        this.lineNumber = lineNumber;\n        this.snippetId = snippetId;\n        this.language = language;\n    }\n\n    toString() {\n        return `Snippet #${this.snippetId} (line ${this.lineNumber}, ${this.language})`;\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Extract code blocks from MDX files.\n */\nexport class MDXCodeExtractor {\n    constructor(mdxPath) {\n        this.mdxPath = mdxPath;\n        this.content = fs.readFileSync(mdxPath, 'utf-8');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Extract all JavaScript/TypeScript code blocks from the MDX file.\n     */\n    extractJavaScriptSnippets() {\n        const snippets = [];\n        \n        // Pattern to match JS/TS code blocks\n        // Use \\b to ensure we don't match \"json\" as \"js\"\n        const pattern = /```(javascript|js|typescript|ts)\\b\\s*\\n(.*?)```/gs;\n        \n        let snippetCount = 0;\n        let match;\n        \n        while ((match = pattern.exec(this.content)) !== null) {\n            const language = match[1];\n            let code = match[2];\n            \n            // Find line number\n            const matchStart = match.index;\n            const lineNumber = this.content.substring(0, matchStart).split('\\n').length;\n            \n            // Clean up code\n            code = this._cleanCode(code);\n            \n            if (!code.trim()) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            \n            snippetCount++;\n            snippets.push(new CodeSnippet(\n                code,\n                lineNumber,\n                snippetCount,\n                language\n            ));\n        }\n        \n        return snippets;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Extract bash code blocks (for npm install commands).\n     */\n    extractBashSnippets() {\n        const snippets = [];\n        const pattern = /```bash\\s*[^\\n]*\\n(.*?)```/gs;\n        \n        let snippetCount = 0;\n        let match;\n        \n        while ((match = pattern.exec(this.content)) !== null) {\n            const code = match[1];\n            const matchStart = match.index;\n            const lineNumber = this.content.substring(0, matchStart).split('\\n').length;\n            \n            // Only include if it has npm install\n            if (code.includes('npm install') || code.includes('npm i ') || code.includes('yarn add')) {\n                snippetCount++;\n                snippets.push(new CodeSnippet(\n                    code,\n                    lineNumber,\n                    snippetCount,\n                    'bash'\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return snippets;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Clean and dedent code.\n     */\n    _cleanCode(code) {\n        let lines = code.split('\\n');\n        \n        // Remove leading/trailing empty lines\n        while (lines.length \u0026\u0026 !lines[0].trim()) {\n            lines.shift();\n        }\n        while (lines.length \u0026\u0026 !lines[lines.length - 1].trim()) {\n            lines.pop();\n        }\n        \n        if (!lines.length) {\n            return '';\n        }\n        \n        // Find minimum indentation\n        let minIndent = Infinity;\n        for (const line of lines) {\n            if (line.trim()) {\n                const indent = line.length - line.trimStart().length;\n                minIndent = Math.min(minIndent, indent);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Remove common indentation\n        if (minIndent !== Infinity \u0026\u0026 minIndent \u003e 0) {\n            lines = lines.map(line =\u003e \n                line.length \u003e minIndent ? line.substring(minIndent) : line\n
